 karat kaa hathkaarat jis shuddhtavaad kii duhai de rahe hai uske paksh main or yechuri ke prastaav ke virodh main unako apane tark paanch baar badalane pade
 The Karat faction did not want to allow Yechury's proposal to pass at any cost and he was also successful in it
 haalanki party kaa teen saal ke antaraal par hone vaala rashtriya adhiveshan abhi yechuri ke paas antim daanv ke taur par bachaa he
 The national convention is going to be held in Hyderabad in April this year and Yechury can make a final effort to get his talk passed
 lekin is antarkalah ne party ko do hisson main to baant hi diya he
 At a time when the party should have made a strong political intervention by broadening its base, along with other parties for consent and cooperation, the party seems to be embroiled in its own differences
 yah bhi vicitra he ki party kaa karat dhada jis shuddhtavaad kii duhai de rahaa he, wo khud usapar tatasth nahin rahaa he
 This purism was called for in 1996 to prevent Jyoti Basu from becoming Prime Minister, but under the leadership of Karat, the party remained part of the UPA
 bharat-america parmaanu samjhaute par upie se alag hone tak chaar saal biit gaye the
 After backing UPA-1 from outside, Karat is again calling for the same purism
 1996 main jyoti basu ko rokna karat or unke saathiyon kii pehali bhul thi
 Does Karat want the Left to not come to power until the people with a clear majority of the Left parties reach Parliament
 kya tabatak badlaav main bina bhagidaar bane keval sangharsh kaa naaraa diya jaataa rahe
 And the question is not only about change
 usase bhi bada sawaal he lagaataar logon ke adhikaron or sansadhano kii ho rahi lut
 To prevent this and to curb anti-people decisions at the policy level, what is the harm if the Left parties come with the ruling parties
 kya karat chaahate hai ki jabatak log sab taraf se harkar satta kii kaman unhen na saunp den, tabatak desh main logon kii adhikaron, jivan or sansadhano se khilwaad hota rahe or desh gart main jaataa rahe
 Jyoti Basu did a fantastic job in Bengal
 wo desh kaa netritv karke ek misaal kaayam kar sakate the
 People had hope from the Left
 raajnneetik prasar main bhi is kadam kaa laabh miltaa
 But nothing like this was stopped
 or ab duusari badi galati kii ja rahi he jo sipiem ko shuddhtavaad kii kuntha se zyaada kuch nahin de sakati
 One of the arguments of the Karat camp is that the Congress has been the main battle in our three Left States
 to kya sipiem ab kshetreey dal ke rup main hi apane ko simit kar chuki he? unke paas rashtriya raajnneeti main dakhal dene or badi raajnneeti ke liye ek vyapak drushti rakhane kii zarurat kya myne nahin rakhti
 Do they not think that in weak opposition politics, the crisis to keep the parties alive is deepening and is the CPM able to stop Modi by taking his book and flag alone? Karat's argument theoretically even Look right, but they lack practicality
 aisa lagata he ki karat abhi bhi jeenyu ke apane chaatr jivan ke daur se baahar nahin nikal paae hai
 In this absence, the student politics of JNU is no more
 vahaan se kanhaiya kumaar, umr khalid or shahala jaise yuva chehre ek vyapak ladaai ke liye apane raajnneetik daayaron ko badhaane main lage hai
 And for the weakening Left, there is no other option in the era of changed politics and more powerful power than ever before
 karat jis raajnneeti kii baat kar rahe hai, uske liye unhen chahie ki wo chunaav aadhaarit vartmaan pranali ko khaarij karke shuddh or saidhantik raajnneetik utthan kii disha main aage badhen
 And then see who among his party or colleagues want to go ahead with him
 communist raajnneeti main namboodripad se lekar surajeet tak kii parampara ko khaarij karke wo apana alag rasta bana sakate hai jaisaa ki vam vichaar ke kuch dal karte rahe hai
 The benefit of this move of Karat is not to anyone but the BJP and the Sangh themselves
 karat bhale hi kerala main unase ladane kaa dam bharte rahen, deshbhar main isse sipiem or vamadalon kii raajnneeti kamazor hi hogi
 The untouchability that has been instilled in the fever of this purism will keep the CPM isolated which is a very negative condition for the party's national role and politics
 vamadalon kii sabase behatar baat yah rahi he ki unke paas baaki raajnneetik dalon se behatar naitik auki saaf-suthri raajnneeti kaa ateet he
 In such a situation, the Left can play its role as one of the most efficient factions to create alternative politics
 vamadalon main abhi bhi wo takat he jiske chalate kai paraspar virdohi dal ekasaath ikattha ho sakate hai or vikalp kii raajnneeti ke liye samvaad shuru kar sakate hai
 This purism of Karat can prove suicidal in this difficult time
 unka hath or ahm vampanthi raajnneeti or khud sipiem ko le dubegaa

 " In the Shivalik area of malviya Nagar, a posh area in south Delhi, a driver attacked 26-year-old fashion designer Kaveri on Sunday afternoon
 asal main anil naam kaa ek shaks jo kareeb ek saal pehle kaveri ke yahan driver kii naukari par tha, use 15 din main naukari se nikaal diya gaya tha, vah ravivaar ko achaanak kaveri ke ghar panhucha or parking se gaadi said karne ke liye kaha 
 He also called Kaveri and asked him to remove the car, after which, as soon as Kaveri came down to the parking lot to remove the car, Anil sat in Kaveri's car and stabbed Kaveri's throat several times
 puri sajeesh ke tahat kaveri ke upar hamalaa kiya gaya haalanki kaveri ne behad bahaduree se anil ko jawaab diya or donon ke bich hathapayee bhi hui, apane makasad main kamyaabi nahin milti dekh anil mauqaa pate hi faraar ho gaya
 a nearby friend admitted Kaveri to the hospital
 tippaniyan This incident was carried out in a very posh area, CCTV cameras are also installed here but till now the accused is out of the police's grip
 ilaake ke log is vaardaat se sahame hue hai
 Kaveri did not have any police verification of the attacker's driver nor did he know his whereabouts
